    WHEN `t0`.`createdAt` >= @__startOfMonth_3 THEN COALESCE(`t0`.`amount`, 0.0)
END), 0.0) AS `RevMonthly`, COALESCE(SUM(COALESCE(`t0`.`amount`, 0.0)), 0.0) AS `RevTotal`
FROM (
    SELECT `t`.`amount`, `t`.`createdAt`, 1 AS `Key`
    FROM `tblOrders` AS `t`
    WHERE (`t`.`isDeleted` IS NULL) OR NOT (`t`.`isDeleted`)
) AS `t0`
GROUP BY `t0`.`Key`
LIMIT 1
